country_event = {
	id = 300008
	title = "Dynamic Loc Region Selection Handler"
	desc = ""
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		change_variable = { which = dynamic_loc_names_region value = 1 }
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					check_variable = { which = dynamic_loc_names_region value = 0.9 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = dynamic_loc_names_region value = 1.1 } }
					check_variable = { which = dynamic_loc_region_count value = 0.9 }
				}
			}

				country_event = {
					id = 300009
					days = 0
				}
			}
		}

			limit = {
				owner = {

					NOT = { check_variable = { which = dynamic_loc_names_region value = 2.1 } }

				}
			}
